 
1)Who is responsible for the virtualization layer down to the physical security of
the facilities in which AWS services operate under the AWS shared
responsibility model?
options
1) It is the sole responsibility of the customer
2) It is the sole responsibility of AWS.
3) It is a shared responsibility between AWS and the customer.
4)The customer's AWS Support plan tier determines who manages the configuration.
Correct answer:
 It is the sole responsibility of AWS.

2) A business is contemplating migrating to the AWS Cloud. The firm wishes to be
able to scale its computing capacity in response to changing demand
conditions.Which AWS Cloud advantage does this case illustrate?
options
1)Global deployments in minutes
2)Cost savings
3)Agility
4)Elasticity
Correct answer :
Elasticity
 
3)What is raised when a business deploys web servers across several AWS
Regions?
options 
1)Coupling
2)Availability
3)Security
4)Durability
 Correct answer:
Availability

4)Which resource is the MOST EFFECTIVE for keeping current on AWS security
announcements?
options
1)AWS Personal Health Dashboard
2)AWS Secrets Manager
3)AWS Security Bulletins
4)Amazon Inspector
Correct answer :
AWS Security Bulletins

5)On an Amazon EC2 instance, a batch job takes 5 hours to complete. Monthly,
the quantity of data to be processed doubles, and the time required to process
it is proportionate.What is the optimal cloud architecture for meeting this
escalating demand?
options
1)Run the application on a bigger EC2 instance size.
2)Switch to an EC2 instance family that better matches batch requirements.
3)Distribute the application across multiple EC2 instances and run the workload in parallel.
4)Run the application on a bare metal EC2 instance.
 Correct answer :
Distribute the application across multiple EC2 instances and run the workload in parallel.

6)Which choices do users have when contacting AWS Support? (Select two.)
options
1)Create an email case in the AWS Support Center.
2)Visit a local AWS Support Center.
3)Use live chat functionality 
4) Use the video conference functionality of the AWS Support console.
Correct answer :
 Create an email case in the AWS Support Center.
Use live chat functionality 

7)A user must locate, categorize, and safeguard sensitive data stored in Amazon

options
1)Amazon Inspector
2) Amazon Macie
3)Amazon GuardDuty
4) AWS Secrets Manager
Correct answer :

8)What is an example of AWS Cloud's high availability?
options
1)Consulting AWS technical support at any time day or night
2)Ensuring an application remains accessible, even if a resource fails
3)Making any AWS service available for use by paying on demand
4)Deploying in any part of the world using AWS Regions
Correct answer :
Ensuring an application remains accessible, even if a resource fails

12)How can a user safeguard against AWS service outages in the event of a
widespread natural disaster?
options
1)Deploy applications across multiple Availability Zones within an AWS Region
2)Use a hybrid cloud computing deployment model within the geographic area.
3)Deploy applications across multiple AWS Regions.
4)Store application artifacts using AWS Artifact and replicate them across multiple AWS Regions.
Correct answer:
Deploy applications across multiple AWS Regions.

14)How might an AWS client implement common access restrictions to a big
group of users easily?
options
1)Apply an IAM policy to an IAM group.
2)Apply an IAM policy to an IAM role.
3)Apply the same IAM policy to all IAM users with access to the same workload.
4)Apply an IAM policy to an Amazon Cognito user pool.
Correct answer :
Apply an IAM policy to an IAM group.

 Correct answer :

25)How can AWS Trusted Advisor assist AWS Cloud users? (Select two.)
options
1)It identifies software vulnerabilities in applications running on AWS
2)It provides a list of cost optimization recommendations based on current AWS usage
3)It detects potential security vulnerabilities caused by permissions settings on account resources
4)It automatically corrects potential security issues caused by permissions settings on account resources
5)It provides proactive alerting whenever an Amazon EC2 instance has been compromised
Correct answer :
It provides a list of cost optimization recommendations based on current AWS usage
It detects potential security vulnerabilities caused by permissions settings on account resources

38)On an Amazon EC2 instance, a business hosts an application. Several AWS
resources, including Amazon S3 and Amazon DynamoDB, are required by the
EC2 instance.What is the MOST OPTIMAL way to delegate permissions?
options
1)Create an IAM role with the required permissions. Attach the role to the EC2 instance.
2)Create an IAM user and use its access key and secret access key in the application.
3)Create an IAM user and use its access key and secret access key to create a CLI profile in the EC2 instance
4)Create an IAM role with the required permissions. Attach the role to the administrative IAM user.
Correct answer :
 Create an IAM role with the required permissions. Attach the role to the EC2 instance.

Security Group acts as a firewall at the instance level whereas Network Access Control List (Network ACL) acts as a firewall at the subnet level
